powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.The Shard</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">碎片大厦（伦敦地标建筑之一,欧洲第二高大厦）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.put off</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">推迟；扔掉；阻止</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：We’ve put off our sports meet because of rain.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">由于下雨，我们不得不推迟运动会。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">put off sb. from doing sth 阻止某人做某事</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.tenant英 /'tenənt/ 美 /'tɛnənt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 承租人；房客；佃户；居住者</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 租借（常用于被动语态）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：The decorating was done by a previous tenant.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">装修是前房客搞的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.dodgy英 /'dɒdʒɪ/ 美 /'dɑdʒi/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 狡猾的，逃避的；善于骗人的；躲闪的；有毛病的；危险的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：If you get any dodgy situations, call me.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果你遇上什么难事，给我打电话。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.optimistic英 /ɒptɪ'mɪstɪk/ 美 /,ɑptɪ'mɪstɪk/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 乐观的；乐观主义的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：I’m cautiously optimistic.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我持谨慎的乐观态度。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">反义词：pessimistic  adj.悲观的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.landmark英 /'læn(d)mɑːk/ 美 /'lændmɑrk/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. [航]陆标；地标；界标；里程碑；纪念碑；地界标；划时代的事</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 有重大意义或影响的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：The world-renowned landmark dates back to the year 70,when construction started.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这座著名的世界级地标性建筑时间可以追溯到公元70年。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.walkie talkie/ walkie-talkie</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.对讲机，携带式无线电话机</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.go up</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">增长；被建造</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：He noticed a new building going up near the park.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他注意到一幢新楼正在公园附近拔地而起。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.grater英 /'greɪtə/ 美 /'ɡretɚ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 摩擦器；磨光机；[木] 粗齿木锉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cheese grater 奶酪刨</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10.crane英 /kreɪn/ 美 /kren/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 吊车，起重机；鹤</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 伸着脖子看；迟疑，踌躇</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 用起重机起吊；伸长脖子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">11.on the scene</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在场；出现；到场</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：Firefighters were on the scene immediately.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">消防队立刻赶到现场。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">back on the scene 重新出现</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">12.skyscraper英 /'skaɪskreɪpə/ 美 /'skaɪ'skrepɚ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 摩天楼，超高层大楼；特别高的东西</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Rob: So, the owner<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: location for business – bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the curren<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> economic situation coul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> be putting off tenants fro<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">m</span></span> moving in.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这么说来，碎片大厦的所有者本想把它建设成办公地点</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">做生意的好位置。但目前的经济形势让租客们无法租赁。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Callum: Yes, he describe<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> the economy as dodgy – a slang word for uncertain or risky.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没错，他形容经济时用到了</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">dodgy</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。这个词是俚语，是不确定的、冒险的意思。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Rob: That's no<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(227, 108, 10);box-sizing: border-box;">the </span></em>view of Boris Johnson, the Mayo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r o</span></span>f London. He's prou<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d o</span></span>f the new building and, together with other new constructions, he's optimistic abou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the future. See i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f y</span></span>ou can hear the name<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s o</span></span>f some other London landmarks that he mentions:</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">伦敦市市长鲍里斯</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">约翰逊并不这么认为。这座大厦及其他新式建筑让他感到很骄傲，他对未来持有乐观的态度。接下来我们再听一段话，看你能否听出他所提到的伦敦其他标志性建筑的名字。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">You've go<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the Walkie Talkie going up, The Cheese Grater, the stuff tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> wasn't happening four year<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span>go, all those cranes stopped moving four years ago; they're bac<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k o</span></span>n the scene now.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们现在有</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">对讲机</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">、</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">奶酪刨</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，我们四年前还没有这些建筑。四年前，所有起重机都停下了工作；现在，它们又回到了施工现场。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Callum: Some interesting names for buildings there – The Walkie Talkie an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> The Cheese Grater! Thi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s i</span></span>s, of course, becau<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">se o</span></span>f the sha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">pe o</span></span>f the buildings, which loo<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">k</span></span> like the objects they are name<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>fter. I suppose these names ma<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ke i</span></span>t easier to identify the buildings.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">他提到了几个有趣的建筑名称，比如对讲机和奶酪刨。它们因其形状而得名，他们看起来与被命名的物体很像。我觉得这些名称让建筑更容易被识别。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Rob: Yes bu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t I</span></span> think I'd be quite embarrasse<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to tell people I work in The Cheese Grater! OK, well it's time now to reveal the answer to today's question.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">那倒是，如果和别人说我在奶酪刨里工作，这会让我感到很尴尬。好了，是时候揭晓本期问题的答案了。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Callum: Ah yes. You as<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">ked</span></span> me, according to the Guinness World Records, the first ever skyscraper was buil<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t i</span></span>n the USA but in which city?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没错，你之前问我，据世界吉尼斯纪录记载，美国第一座摩天大楼建在哪个城市？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">SHASTA ran lightly along the roof on tiptoes. It felt hot to his bare feet. He was only a few seconds scrambling up the wall at the far end and when he got to the corner he found himself looking down into a narrow, smelly street, and there was a rubbish heap against the outside of the wall just as Corin had told him. Before jumping down he took a rapid glance round him to get his bearings. Apparently he had now come over the crown of the island-hill on which Tashbaan is built.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">沙斯塔踮起脚尖沿着屋顶轻轻地跑去，觉得他的光脚丫子发烫。不到几秒钟他就爬到了墙垣的另一头，他到了墙角，俯瞰一条狭窄、发臭的小街，正如科林告诉他的，墙外有个垃圾堆。跳下去之前，他先向周围迅速地扫了一眼，以便认清方位。显而易见，他已经来到塔什班岛城的山顶上了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：乔，你今天能给我挤出点时间来吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：这可够呛，珍妮。我的确忙不开。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我明白你的意思。可我必须得在去见收税的之前跟你过一遍账。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：好吧，让我想想怎么办。1:30怎么样？在我午餐会议之后。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：好的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Joe, can you squeeze me in sometime today?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That’s a big order, Jane. I am really swamped.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I know what you’re saying, but I have to go over the books with you before I go see our tax guy.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Right. Okay, let me see what I can do. How about 1:30 right after my lunch meeting?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: OK.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Expect the best, plan for the worst, and prepare to be surprised.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抱最好的期望，做最坏的__________，并准备接受意外的惊喜。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">打算</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">山区的野生动物也面临危险。中亚的雪豹、维龙加的山地大猩猩、不丹的孟加拉皇家虎和其他物种无不因周边更广泛的生态系统变化和人类对地貌景观的利用而受到影响，进而可能向纵深侵蚀偏远和高海拔地区，并加剧人与野生动物的冲突。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Mountain wildlife is also at risk. Snow leopards in Central Asia, mountain gorillas in Virunga, Royal Bengal tigers in Bhutan and other species are affected by changes to wider ecosystems and human uses of the landscape that could, in turn, lead to further encroachment into remote and high-altitude areas and increased human-wildlife conflict.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">许渊冲老先生于昨日仙逝。他</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一生勤奋，留下许多优秀的翻译作品。我本人非常敬重他，也很喜欢他的翻译，也因此大家经常能在推送里看到“许渊冲 译”这几个字。</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">感谢许渊冲先生，</strong><span style='box-sizing: border-box;font-weight: 700;user-select: text;-webkit-user-drag: none;-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", "Apple Color Emoji", "Emoji Symbols Font", "Segoe UI Symbol", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 14px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);'>创作出那么多让大家喜爱的翻译作品。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style='box-sizing: border-box;font-weight: 700;user-select: text;-webkit-user-drag: none;-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", "Apple Color Emoji", "Emoji Symbols Font", "Segoe UI Symbol", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 14px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);'><br/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我总结了公众号里用许老翻译作品所制作的早读和为你读诗节目，以此纪念许先生。点击图片即可跳转。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">许渊冲先生，一路走好！</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section to sb (that)...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">浮现于脑中，被想起，被想到</strong></p><p style="white-space: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我突然意识到</strong>，这些希望是有一定的主题的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">To that point,<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">it occurs to me</strong></em></span> that we might have an opportunity.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说到这一点，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我突然想到</strong>我们也许有机会。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5539305" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《The Big Bang Theory》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">by something或doing sth </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">方式状语，通过...，后接</strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">名词或动名词形式</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">obtain verb. 获得，赢得</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I finally managed to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">obtain </strong></em></span>a copy of the report.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我终于设法<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">弄到了</strong>这份报告的一个副本。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You will need to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">obtain </strong></em></span>permission from the principal.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你需要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">得到</strong>校长的同意。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...a means by which to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">obtain </strong></em></span>the blood.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一种能够<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">获得</strong>血的手段。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《犯罪心理》</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We were able to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">obtain </strong></em></span>Krick's phone records.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们成功<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">取得</strong>克里克的电话记录。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6179159" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdOd7ZOFsqlF7V5MIiadkH8paIZ60GrVgybRG4p3xGFugmiaFLCSFn5MTWc5I4H43LNQz2m7187xgnQ/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="547" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> it occurs to sb (that)...   </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. tower </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ˈtaʊə/ US/ˈtaʊər/ verb </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to be very tall or large, usually in a way that makes people feel respect高耸，矗立</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: We turned the corner and there was the cathedral, towering in front of us.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们转过拐角，便看见大教堂高高耸立在面前。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">phrasal verb:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">tower above/over sb/sth: to be very tall in comparison with someone or something else</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比…高；矗立在…上</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: Although he's only twelve, David towers over his mother.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然戴维只有12岁，他已经比妈妈高了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">tower above/over sth: to be much bigger and more successful than another thing of the same type比…优秀；远胜于</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: One computer manufacturer towers above all the rest.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一家计算机制造商在同行中一枝独秀。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Idiom: a tower of strength (noun)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a person who gives you help and support when you are in a difficult situation</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（危难时的）可依靠的人，支柱</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: Andrea was a tower of strength to me when I was ill.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我生病时，安德莉娅就是我的精神支柱。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. storey  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/ˈstɔːri/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a level of a building 楼层，层</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a three-storey house 3层高的房子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. Not much of </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">意思是：“不太、不大、不怎么”。在美式口语中，not much of的使用频率很高，它是一种常用的表示委婉否定的方法。much of，意思是”比较多的，偏多的”，而前面添加一个not，则是：”不怎么的”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: I am sure it would be good, however, honestly, I am not much of a fan of fantasy films.我相信这部电影应该不错。但老实说，我其实对奇幻类电影不太感冒/我其实并非奇幻类电影的拥趸。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: He’s not much of an actor really. 他其实算不上/称不上是演员。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. by today's standards 按照现在的标准</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">skyscrapers</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">摩天大楼</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I suppose we could call them skyscrapers – because they're so tall they almost touch the sky.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得可以把它们称作摩天大楼，因为它们几乎快高到天边了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a shard</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">碎片</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">From a distance, with the sun reflecting on it, it looks like a shard – or a sharp, broken piece of glass, which is what a shard means.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在阳光的反射下，它从远处来看就像是碎片，或者说像锋利的碎玻璃片，shard的意义就在于此。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">forking out</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">支付，花钱</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And if you don't mind forking out lots of money you can go to the viewing platform on the 72nd floor for a birds-eye view of the city.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">而且如果你不嫌贵的话，那么你可以前往第72层的观景台去俯瞰整座城市。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the wow factor</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">令人印象深刻的，让人叫好的东西</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The Shard seems to have the wow factor for those people.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这些人似乎对碎片大厦很满意。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">landmark</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">地标，标志性建筑</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Someone else mentioned it was much higher than the London Eye – that's another famous landmark.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有人提到碎片大厦比伦敦眼高更高——另一座著名的标志性建筑。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">prosperous</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">繁荣的，繁华的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's an image that is seen all around the world and it can show a city as being prosperous and modern.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它是世界公认的城市形象，是城市繁荣、现代化的标志。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">observation deck</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">观景台</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Most contain luxury living accommodation, a hotel, offices, and, of course, an observation deck – that's a viewing platform.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大多大厦里都有豪华生活设施、酒店、办公室，当然还有观景台。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">leased</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">租用的，租赁的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">At the moment only 20% of the office space is leased – which means only 20% is rented out. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">到目前为止，只有20%的办公空间被租用。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">established</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">既定的，确定的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What they are trying to do is create an entire quarter here, to make it into more of an established office location but, you know, maybe if you're a tenant, economy's very dodgy, that added bit of risk, maybe that will put people off.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们想在这里开发出一片区域，把它建设成办公地点，但如果你是租户，你知道经济很多变，这会带来风险，让人们对这里望而生畏。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">dodgy</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不可靠的，冒险的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yes, he said described the economy as dodgy – a slang word for uncertain or risky.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没错，他形容经济时用到了dodgy。这个词是俚语，是不确定的、冒险的意思。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Everything sloped away before him, flat roofs below flat roofs, down to the towers and battlements of the city's Northern wall. Beyond that was the river and beyond the river a short slope covered with gardens. But beyond that again there was something he had never seen the like of - a great yellowish-grey thing, flat as a calm sea, and stretching for miles. On the far side of it were huge blue things, lumpy but with jagged edges, and some of them with white tops. "The desert! the mountains!" thought Shasta.  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一切都在他面前迤逦而下，平坦屋顶下方又有平坦屋顶，一直接连到北城城墙及其塔楼和维蝶。城墙外是河流，河流外是一个遍布花园的短坡。再过去便是他从来没看见过有什么跟它类似的景象——灰黄色，平坦得像个平静的海，绵亘好多英里。它的遥远边缘上是大块大块蓝色，凹凹凸凸，参差不齐，有些顶上是雪白的。”大沙漠！大山大岭！！”沙斯塔心里想道。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：卡麦克尔先生，又是我，爱伦·鲍华。您让我这个星期打电话和您定一个面试时间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：是这样，鲍华女士。你好。我不敢肯定这星期能否有时间见你，很难说。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我能理解，卡麦克尔先生。我很愿意安排在下个星期。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：好吧。那我们就定在下周二上午11:30如何？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：好的，谢谢。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Mr. Carmichael, this is Ellen Bower calling again. You had said I should call this week to schedule an interview with you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That’s right, Ms. Bower. How are you? I’m not sure if I’ll be able to fit you in this week, I’m afraid.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I understand, Mr. Carmichael. I’d be glad to make it some time next week.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: All right, then. Why don’t we say next Tuesday at 11:30 a.m.?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: OK, thanks.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Let our ___________ worrying become advance thinking and planning.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">把事前忧虑花的时间，用在事前的思索与准备上。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">advance</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中方支持联合国举办生物多样性峰会，赞赏联合国一直以来在推动全球环境治理进程所作努力和贡献。在全球生物多样性丧失加速、疫情对经济社会带来全面冲击的背景下，各方更应携手合作，共同应对全球生物多样性面临的严峻挑战。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">China supports the United Nations in holding the Biodiversity Summit and lauds the UN efforts and contributions in advancing global environmental governance. Against the backdrop of accelerated global biodiversity loss and the impact of COVID-19 on various aspects of the economy and society, it is imperative that all parties work together to address the serious challenges facing global biodiversity.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section Because we only go round once, and when it's over, it's over.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">only go round once 在文中的含义为：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 只走一圈   B 只运转一次   C 只活一次</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653551552&amp;idx=2&amp;sn=3de2ea183114344abfa5a9cc70133913&amp;chksm=f7e83b0dc09fb21b545eb127301f0217029dc2c937ac3a296b847dd4bd260b5f3dbc491bae3c&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="5. It occurs to me you could solve all your problems by obtaining more money.">5. It occurs to me you could solve all your problems by obtaining more money.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">该句中最多包含几处连读？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 2   B 3   C 4 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: left;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本周知识点回想</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.    培养一种友谊感</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.    她百感交集，激动不已。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.    这把椅子挡着我。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.    女孩们每走一步都在咯咯地笑。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.    要想谱写新篇章，就要去探索未知的世界。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.    吃一堑，长一智。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.    道歉方是上策。</p><p style="margin:
